					has_government = democratic
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {

						}
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = SPR
						}
						OR = {
							original_tag = ITA

							original_tag = YUG
							original_tag = ALB
							original_tag = GRE
							original_tag = TUR
							original_tag = CRO
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = generic.5 hours = 6 random_hours = 6 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_puppet = no
						is_in_faction = no
						has_capitulated = no
						OR = {
							has_government = fascism
							has_government = neutrality
						}
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = SPR
						}
						OR = {
							original_tag = ITA

						}
					}

				}
			}
		}
	}
